  subtitle: Second Order Effects
  type: video
  author: Austin Chadwick and Chris Lucian
  layout: post
---

<iframe width="200" height="113" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/AmoeA_Hz5Rg?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen title="Second Order Effects"></iframe>

Chris Lucian and Austin Chadwick discuss all things agile and product development from a mob programming perspective. In this episode Chris and Austin discuss second order effects in systems thinking and the dramatic impact it has on product development and mob programming. Every person in a system who makes a decision has a desired positive effect. However, what are the side effects of that effect and what are the side effects of the side effects? Are they negative or positive? Experiences and suggestions are shared in regards to the second order effects of \"efficient\" code reviews, sprints, metrics, estimates, working solo, etc.

https://podcasts.apple.com/us/podcast/second-order-effects/id1485950034?i=1000487597853

Chris Lucian is the Director of Software Development at Hunter Industries and a founder of mob programming. https://www.chrislucian.com/p/chris-lucian-biography.html 

Austin Chadwick is a Mob Programmer at Hunter Industries and is a passionate agilist and craftsman with experience in several roles (e.g. coach, developer, tester, scrum master, business analyst). www.linkedin.com/in/austin-chadwick-3a58151a4
